 The Duckworth Lewis Rule According to the Duckworth Lewis Rule (D / L), this rule is calculated on the basis of the remaining wickets and overs of the two means used by both teams to score runs in a match with a defined over
 yah niyam antarrashtriya cricket parishad dwaara manyata praapt he

 italy ke abhiyojak dwaara daakhil kii gayi report main idies imphotech kaa naam saamne aayaa

 company ne sabhi aaropon se inkaar kiya he

 loksabhaa chunaav 2019 ke tahat rajasthan kii rajsamand loksabhaa seat par bhartiya janata party kii pratyaashee diya kumari ne congress ummidavaar devakinandan urf kaaka ko 551916 voton ke antar se haraa diya he
 a total of 10 candidates were in the fray here
 haalanki mukhya muqabla bijepi or congress ke bich hi rahaa

 vahiin, unke najdiki pratidwandi congress ke devakinandan urf kaaka 311123 voton ke saath duusare sthaan par hai

 bataa den ki is seat par chauthe charan ke tahat 29 april ko matdaan hua tha or matdaan kaa pratishat 64
 Remained 67
 kin ummidavaaron main tha muqablacongress ne is seat se devakinandan urf kaaka ko tikat diya tha

 2014 kaa chunaav2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav main rajsamand seat par 57

 4 percent votes were cast

 saamaajik taana-banaloksabhaa rajsamand, paali, ajmer or nagaur jile main faili he

 nagaur jile kii medta or degana, ajmer kii beawar or paali jile kii jaitaaran vidhansabha seat shaamil he
